112399007076904054363< /UserId.>
< username>
Eric Sztanyo< /username>
< date>
1465358871870< /date>
< Rating>
5<//Rating>
< review>
Friendly service. Yummy food. Awesome location.

Attending a seminar in San Diego, my wife and I had a brief lunch break. Look, we get to stare at the Ohio River all year. So, instead of hanging around the hotel and conference room any longer, we made a dash to Coronado.

Maybe it's not big deal for the locals, but us mid-westerners need to gobble up ocean views whenever we can!

And, we needed to gobble up some viddles. So, my wife pulls out Yelp on the way, and we the safe bet - go with the highest rated restaurant on Coronado ... there's a reason why.

It was Sunday afternoon. The weather wasn't great, a bit cloudy, so the Islander wasn't slammed. But, we were greeted by a wonderful hostess/waitress, who was extremely friendly. First, she told me I didn't need to pay the meter (which I had missed), then, she knew we were in a hurry and got our fish and chips order in right away. While it was getting ready, she prepped us to go with to go cups and the bill.

When the food came out, the chef (owner?), gave us a pro tip and said, "hey, it's fried. The sooner you open these styrofoam containers, the better it will be." Now, I should know that after years of takeout, but what a friendly and thoughtful tip! This guys was saying, "my food is really good. Here's how to get the most out of it if you are getting it to go."

And, it was delicious! The curry ketchup on the fries ... awesome! My wife hates ketchup, and she gobbled it all up. The horeradish tartar sauce, yum! The cod was fantastic and the pumpkin seed slaw great on the side.

A little pricey for what we normally pay ... but, that comes with the territory on Coronado. If you're going to pay premium, get the best. Go to the Islander!< /review>

Beautiful park, nice grass, has aplay structure we didn't use, but a dad and his kids were enjoying it. We played hackey on the bball court. Bathrooms were locked, no drinking fountains. Presumably so that people who don't own or rent a home can't relieve themselves in the privacy of a restroom with a toilet or wash their hands in a sink when finished. Probably no fountains so that same said people don't have access to water as this might make drug use, hygiene or laundry too easy. But at least everyone else who walks their dogs have plenty of grass for them to deficate upon. Why not have bathrooms for kids/parents and separate ones for adults.</text>

This is a good park to take kids for a nice time. Besides swings and a small play are, there is an unique play area that the kids really enjoyed climbing on and sliding down. There is also a basketball court and a large grassy area that the kids can run around and kick a ball. It's well maintained and sits in a residential area with lots of parking around it. We will visit again. The only thing I did not like, no doors on the bathroom stalls.</review>

<Review>Lovely service; the chef came out several times personally to check on our meal.  Our waiter was relatively attentive and refilled side dishes and beverages briskly.

Tteokbokki was only so-so, will likely try a pajun next time.

Galbi jjim was delicious though; loved how they cut the beef to get more sauce on the surfaces.  Tendon pieces were unexpected, but flavorful.
Galbi sauce was great consistency and went well with the purple rice.   Would have appreciated more quantity though.

Outdoor dining is not recommended for a date night. <user>107974392234770111395<//user><username>Kenneth Trommler</username><Date>1519911531701<//Date>< Rate>

< Review>
So this review is a tough one because the rooms here are really nice. They aren't huge but they come with an iron,blow dryer,fridge,microwave and even a coffee maker. The beds are super comfy and the rooms are decorated very nicely. Consisting of the bed, a nice writing desk and a chair with an ottoman. The sound walls are insulated well keeping heat or cold in and sound out. During the week you can pretty much show up at any hour and get room on the weekends due to its vicinity to the old town bars it gets pretty full. All the rooms at the location are non smoking and they do not allow pets of any kind. My main issue with this place is the random rates they quote you and the weird amounts of tax they charge. (Weekday rate is anywhere from 55 to 99 dollars. Weekend rates are from 110 to 200 a night) The prices are made up on the spot and change day to day even if you are the only guest. Be prepared to threaten to go to the Motel 6 across the street to get the best price for the night. Check out is 11AM if you want a late check out be prepared to fork out 20 dollars an hour. I've been staying at this little inn for several years and if you can get over the haggling and random charges it's a nice room within miles of the wineries, bars and casino. I say check it out if you're in town.</Review>

< text>
NOT bad at all at this local Filipino and supposedly 'fusion' American-Filipino restaurant.  Depending on which platter you get, it ranges about $40 to $50 for 4 to 6 people.   We got the grilled meat platter and all of them were good and made fresh. I also tried their lumpia and it is my least favorite (sorry). The boneless bangus balls (Kind of like meatballs But made of fish) was really good too and the rest of the grilled meat.  You might wanna come before the rush hour or weekdays because there's not much parking.

3 things:
1. I will come back again
2. Grilled liempo is a must
3. Dine-in or To-go  It's to-go!< /text>

< review>
Pinoy Food run

Green Banana Leaf is a new Filipino/Asian Fusion eatery. However, unlike most Filipino food spots in the area, GBL is a sit down restaurant, with a chic d√©cor, 90's hip hop/R&B playing on the house speakers and Instagram worthy dishes. Not a turo-turo (hot tray, point at what you want) place. Being hipster-ish, prices are higher than the typical Filipino haunts. For our inaugural visit, we were in a hurry and shared two plates.

Molo soup
Wow, look at all those wontons! I counted over a dozen wontons by the time we got to the bottom of this huge bowl of soup. Perfect on a cold evening! I could taste the ginger, garlic & onions with every steaming spoonful. I wanted soup (of some sort) and this didn't disappoint.

Quarter chicken combo w/ egg rolls
GBL has various fried chicken combos. We chose the quarter chicken combo, which comes with lumpianitas (egg rolls) and choice of steamed rice or garlic fried rice. The lumpianitas were perfectly fried, crunchy & delicious. I usually don't order chicken from restaurants, as I prefer Church's and avoid chicken everywhere else, but the quarter chicken had a deliciously fried crispy skin. However, the portions were rather meager, so I probably wouldn't order their chicken combo again.

Green Banana Leaf has lunch specials during the week, and their extensive menu has a little something for everyone. I was told by the attendant that their most popular dish is their crispy kare kare, which is a combo of their crispy pata (fried pork hock) & kare kare (peanut butter stew). Being a little less than $20, it would have to wait for us, as we weren't looking to stay too long.

Service was good. The staff were friendly & hospitable, quick with refills. Ample seating via tables in the middle and booths around the perimeter. There is also bar seating, as well.

Parking is at the Fresh Catch Supermarket center. Green Banana Leaf is the last business on the left, next to Caf√© 86.

Green Banana Leaf is a welcome addition to the neighborhood. The food is definitely on point, and I'm eager to try one of their signature dishes, like the crispy kare kare. Although their prices are higher than I'd want to spend on my ancestral cuisine, having lunch specials is enough to lure me back again & again. "What's for dinner?" is never a concern when there's Green Banana Leaf nearby.

Highly recommend!
NOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOM< /review>

<name>Kelley Luna<//name><rating>4< /rating>< Review>
Overcharged CA Cannibis excise tax on my purchases.  A $33.00 total purchase price was $45.79 after taxed were computed.  Current excise tax rate is 15% on all cannibis products sold in CA.  The amount charged s/b $4.95 on $33.00 not $7.21.  CA state law requires that any excess excise tax collected must be refunded to the retail customer who paid the tax.  I will be continuing to make purchases here as I asume there is a simple explanation or a calculation error was made.  Overall this place has great service and great product.  The budtenders and other staff will make your visit a pleasant one.< /Review>

<resp>None< /resp><Date>1621634324651<//Date><Rate>5</Rate><UserId.>107650390783390871917< /UserId.><Review>FIRST TIME EATER!

Went on a work lunch with 2 other amazing ladies to Sushi Yama today - first time ever going here even though its literally walking distance from my office. However I will TOTALLY be back.

We had amazing service from Amber. She was super attentive and nice, quick, efficient and catered to any request we had.

The food was AMAZING! I eat pretty healthy and so I am always aware that I could easily eat 15 sushi rolls and be stoked about it but I need to be strategic.

Their menu is online and was available for me to check out prior to arriving. I knew exactly what I wanted and it came out even better than I anticipated.

I am not sure why I haven't been there before but it will definitely be a return.

It was so delicious I literally just asked my husband if he wanted to go tonight on a date night!

5 out of 5 would definitely recommend!

- Masks to and from tables
- Casual environment
- Will be an epic summer eatery as they keep it really cold in their due to food that they serve (I recommend a jacket if you run cold)
- No outside smokers air comes in
- Split tab friendly
- Great service
- Very reasonably priced
- Indoor and patio seating
- Attached parking lot (its across the street from City Hall's larger lot)< /Review><Pics>None<//Pics>< Gmap_id>

<userid>104485078818799754403< /userid><Name>Frank Tupas</Name><time>1567004738109<//time><rating>5</rating>< review>
Very nice sushi restaurant in Escondido. Appreciated the service the most but the food was good and they offered 50% off rolls. We started with the Pan Fried Gyozs which is basically dumplings with sesame ponzu which came out fast and was so good!!

For rolls we got a bunch and they were all good!!! We got the (1) Escondido (my favorite) which was shrimp tempura, crab, cucumber, tuna, salmon, eel, avo, topped with spicy aioli, eel sauce, & potato crunches; (2) The Centipede which was shrimp tempura, spicy tuna, cucumber, topped with avocado & balsamic glaze; (3) Orange County which was spicy crab, cucumber, topped with salmon, avocado, and yuzu essence, and finally a standard crunchy roll which was shrimp tempura, crab, cucumber, tempura flakes and soy glaze

If I had any complaint it would be that the rolls weren't rolled very well so they fall apart big time but the taste, service, and reasonable price will get me to go back there< /review>
